<rating>2</rating>< text>
Sooooo... we were thirsty and wanted to take our masks off.  It was late afternoon and this place was open right off of Hollywood Blvd. touristy area.  Before we were allowed in, a guy wearing a mask that did not cover his nose was schooling us on where we had to where a mask inside.  But like I said, we were thirsty and the place was not busy (which we liked) so we went in anyway.  We ordered 2 beers - the IPA and Lager on tap.  As you can see from the photo... which I had yet to take a drink... the Lager was filled up HALF way.  Maybe 2/3rds of the way at best.  It was so bizarre.  I was not in the mood to get into a confrontation, maybe that is how they do it here?  The IPA was full up, with a nice head.  The guy literally pulling the beer could not have missed that he was giving me a 60% full glass.  $16 bucks for them both.

BUT I give them 2 stars because the vibe inside was cool... very airy and plenty of spacing.  Clean bathrooms.  Obviously we only had one drink!< /text>

< Text>
Fig Mtn was one of my first loves, when I got into craft beer, back around 6-7 years ago. The Buellton location was at the time the only location. During that time I was responsible for getting Fig into a golf course in Oxnard, called River Ridge GC. Ive since been a fan, and recently visited the Los Olivos location. To my surprise, we saw Hana!!!! She was one of our first bartenders at the Buellton location, and it was so nice to see that she is still part of the family! Hana has a beautiful spirit about here, a warming comfort, welcoming vibe. Be sure to look for her!< /Text>

< text>
Fig Mountain's oasis of beer in a town of tasting rooms. Beer on tap is a sampling of what's available at the larger tap rooms. Staff are busy, but on point, though it's so cramped when busy not much they can do. They have enough seating, air conditioning, and a real bathroom to make this a genuine tourist destination.

Parking is Los Olivos standard malarkey, but there's a bathroom! A real bathroom! Beer's good too.</text>

I chose Everbloom Flowers to send my sister who lives in San Diego a gift for her birthday.  I looked at multiple floral business in her area but it was Everbloom that stood far far above the rest!  Beautiful website, easy to navigate, check out process was streamlined and when I called to let them know to delete something on the order, I was greeted by a cheerful gentleman!  You know how some florists have pictures and you choose the arrangement you'd like to send and when it gets to its destination, it's not even close to the picture?  Not with Everbloom Flowers ... this floral arrangement was EXTRAORDINARY!  I received a pic from my sister and the arrangement was HUGE, the vase was exactly the same as shown with pink ribbon, and the floral arrangement itself was tall and gorgeous and delivered when said.

< review>
Another one of those places we just found by accident. It's actually got a concrete bathroom, which is very nice! And you know anywhere that has a danger warning sign when you first pull up is going to be really really cool hahaha but this place is unbelievable when the tie-dye the beach disappears and then it low tide you can walk through so come and have a great time. Also if you happen to have a dog? The seagulls love this beach and the dogs love to make them fly which is actually pretty entertaining if you enjoy that kind of stuff haha<//review>
